<S n="2500">
<s>tarasA ye na Sakyante SastrEH suniSitErapi .</s>
<s>sAmnA te 'pi nigfhyante gajA iva kareRuBiH ..</s>
</S>
<D n="2500" a="4108">
<b>2500.</b> (<b>4108.</b>) Selbst diejenigen, die
nicht durch Gewalt, auch nicht durch die
schärfsten Waffen bezwungen werden
können, werden durch Güte bezwungen, wie
(wilde) Elephanten durch
Elephantenweibchen.
</D>
<F n="2500">
2500) MBH. 12, 5172.
</F>
</entry>

<s>vfdDasya maraRacintA anekacintA daridrasya ..</s>
</S>
<D n="2501">
<b>2501.</b> Ein Jüngling denkt an Liebe, ein
Mann an Reichthümer, ein Greis an den
Tod, ein Armer an Vielerlei.

<info L="2502" page="2.58" gtypes="S,D,F"/>
<S n="2502">
<s>taruRimasamAramBe tasyAH SarIrasarovaraM</s>
<s>saraBasa manohaMsa SrImanprayAsi kaTaM punaH .</s>
<s>SravaRalatikApASO pArSve prasAritapAtitO</s>
<s>hataviDivaSAdbanDAyAnDo na paSyati kiM BavAn ..</s>
</S>
<D n="2502" a="4109">
<b>2502.</b> (<b>4109.</b>) Wie kommt es, dass beim
Beginn ihrer ersten Jugend du, o Herz,
ein ungestümer schöner Flamingo, zum
prächtigen See, ihrem Leibe, dich immer
und immer wieder begiebst? Siehst du
denn nicht, o Blinder, weil das böse
Schicksal es so will, die zur Seite
ausgespannten und hingeworfenen
Schlingen, jene Schlingpflanzen, die
Ohren?
</D>
<F n="2502">
2502) ŚĀNTIŚ. in NĪTISAṂK. 77.
fg. ŚATAKĀV. 33 und in der Tüb.
Hdschr. ²a. <s>taruRaviSamAramBe</s>. ²b.
<s>SrImAn; mama</s> st. <s>punaH</s>.

</F>

<D n="2503" a="105">

<D n="2504">

«zu viel» hat man nirgends gern.

Demüthigungen, Dummköpfe hasst sie, zu
gar grossen Gelehrten fühlt sie keine
Zuneigung, auch fürchtet sie sich sehr
vor Heldenmüthigen und ganz Feige
verlacht sie, o Weh!
</D>

<S n="2636">
<s>tyAjyaM na DEryaM viDure 'pi dEve DEryAtkadAcitsTitimApnuyAtsaH .</s>
<s>jAte samudre 'pi hi potaBaNge sAMyAtriko vAYCati pArameva ..</s>
</S>
<D n="2636" a="172">
<b>2636.</b> (<b>172.</b>) Man darf den Muth nicht
sinken lassen, auch wenn das Schicksal
widerwärtig sein sollte, da man durch
Standhaftigkeit über kurz oder lang eine
feste Stellung erlangen kann. Wünscht
doch ein Seefahrer, wenn ihm auch im
Meere ein Schiffbruch widerfahren ist,
seinen Bestimmungsort zu erreichen.
</D>
<F n="2636">
2636) PAÑCAT. ed. KOSEG. I, 220. ed.
Bomb. 316. ²a. <s>kAle</s> st. <s>dEve</s>
ed. Bomb. ²b. <s>tatim</s> st. <s>sTitim</s>
ed. Bomb. ²c. <s>jAte</s> unsere Aenderung
für <s>yAte</s> der KOSEG. Ausg., ed. Bomb.
liest st. dessen <s>yaTA</s> und ausserdem
<s>ca</s> st. <s>hi</s>. ²d. <s>karma eva</s> st.
<s>sArameva</s> KOSEG.; in der 1 ten
Auflage war statt dessen <s>tartumeva</s>
vermuthet worden, welches jetzt auch in
der ed. Bomb. erscheint. Da wir aber aus
einer mündlichen Aeusserung BÜHLER's
wissen, dass die Herausgeber der Bomb.
Ausg. einige Conjecturen von uns in
ihren Text aufgenommen haben, so dürfen
wir auf diese Uebereinstimmung kein
grosses Gewicht legen. <s>pArameva</s> war
shcon in den Nachträgen in der 1ten
Auflage als passender bezeichnet worden,
wobei auf Spruch <s>Darma eva plavo
nAnyaH</s> verwiesen wurde.
</F>

<D n="2643" a="4147">
<b>2643.</b> (<b>4147.</b>) Viṣṇu, der Herr der
drei Welten, ward zur Zielscheibe der
Pfeile eines wilden Bergbewohners; der
Schöpfer der Welten (Brahman) musste es
leiden, dass ihm ein Haupt abgeschlagen
wurde; Sonne und Mond da wurden ein
Bissen Rāhu's; der mächtige Śiva ist
nackt; wer vermag über das hinweg zu
kommen, was ihm an die Stirn geschrieben
wurde?
</D>

<info L="2647,2648,2649,2650,2651" page="2.89" gtypes="S,S,S,S,S,D,D,D,D,D,F"/>
<S n="2647">
<s>triviDAH puruzA loke uttamADamamaDyamAH .</s>
<s>tezAM tu samavetAnAM guRadozO vadAmyaham ..</s>
</S>
<S n="2648">
<s>mantrastriBirhi saMyuktaH samarTErmantranirRaye .</s>
<s>mitrErvApi samAnArTErbAnDavErapi vADikEH ..</s>
</S>
<S n="2649">
<s>sahito mantrayitvA yaH karmAramBAnpravartayet .</s>
<s>dEve ca kurute yatnaM tamAhuH puruzottamam ..</s>
</S>
<S n="2650">
<s>eko 'rTaM vimfSedeko Darme prakurute manaH .</s>
<s>ekaH kAryARi kurute tamAhurmaDyamaM naram ..</s>
</S>
<S n="2651">
<s>guRadozO na niScitya tyaktvA dEvavyapASrayam .</s>
<s>karizyAmIti yaH kAryamupekzetsa narADamaH ..</s>
</S>
<D n="2647">
<b>2647.</b> Es giebt in der Welt Diener von
dreierlei Art: ausgezeichnete, schlechte
und mittelmässige; die Vorzüge und
Mängel aller dieser drei will ich dir
nun verkünden.
</D>
<D n="2648">
<b>2648.</b> Eine Berathung findet mit Dreien
Statt: mit solchen, die einen Plan zu
machen im Stande sind, mit Freunden, die
einen gleichen Zweck verfolgen, oder mit
überlegenen Verwandten.
</D>
<D n="2649">
<b>2649.</b> Wer sich nun mit diesen beräth,
bevor er an ein Werk geht, und wer auf
das Schicksal die gehörige Rücksicht
nimmt, den nennt man einen
ausgezeichneten Diener.
</D>
<D n="2650">
<b>2650.</b> Wer eine Sache allein erwägt,
allein seinen Sinn auf das Rechte
richtet und allein die Angelegenheiten
vollbringt, den nennt man einen
mittelmässigen Diener.
</D>
<D n="2651">
<b>2651.</b> Wer sich nicht vom Vortheil oder
Nachtheil einer Sache überzeugt, es
versäumt auf das Schicksal Rücksicht zu
nehmen und ein Geschäft vernachlässigt,
indem er bei sich denkt, er werde es
schon vollbringen, den nennt man einen
schlechten Diener.
</D>
<F n="2647,48,49,50,51">
2647.48.49.50.51) R. ed. Bomb. 6, 6, 6.
<pb n="2.90"/> fgg. ed. GORR. 5, 77, 7.
fgg. Bei GORR. folgende Abweichungen:
2647, ²d. <s>°dozAn</s>. 2648, ²a.
<s>mantriBirhatasaMyuktEH</s>. ²b.

<s>saha saMmantrya yo mantraM</s>. ²b.

matim</s>. 2651, ²a. ²b.

gleichgiltig gegen Alles.

<info L="2655" page="2.91" gtypes="S,D,F,V5"/>
<S n="2655">
<s>tvaM cetsaMcarase vfzeRa laGutA kA nAma digdantinAM</s>
<s>vyAlEH kaNkaRaBUzaRAni kuruze hAnirna hemnAmapi .</s>
<s>mUrDanyaM kuruze sitAMSumayaSaH kiM nAma lokatrayI-</s>
<s>dIpasyAmbujabAnDavasya jagatAmISo 'si kiM brUmahe ..</s>
</S>
<D n="2655" a="179">
<b>2655.</b> (<b>179.</b>) Wenn du (Śiva) auf einem
Stiere reitest, warum sollten die
welttragenden Elephanten geringgeachtet
werden? Wenn du aus Schlangen bestehende
Armbänder anlegst, lässt man darum das
Gold nicht fahren; wenn du den
Weissstrahligen (den Mond) als Diadem
auf dem Kopfe trägst, sollte darum die
Leuchte der Dreiwelt (die Sonne), die
Freundin der am Tage blühenden
Wasserrosen, zur Unehre kommen? Doch was
reden wir, da du der Herr der Welten
bist?
</D>
<F n="2655">
2655) KUVALAY. 161, ²a. ²c. Dem
Commentator scheint die Lesart
<s>jalAMSum = jaqAMSum</s> st. <s>sitAMSum</s>
vorgelegen zu haben.
</F>

-- 2655. ŚĀRṄGADHARA. ²b. <s>kAYcanakuRqalAni</s> und <s>hemnaH punaH</s>. ²c. <s>mUrDnA cedvahase jaqAMSum</s> und <s>lokatraye</s>.

ausgerissen wurden. Was hat der Schöpfer
nicht Alles zusammenketten müssen, um
einem durch die Gewalt eines Sturmwindes
entwurzelten Baume, der, ich weiss nicht
woher, angeflogen kam, in jener (vom

<D n="2685" a="4159">
<b>2685.</b> (<b>4159.</b>) Wenn dem Schöpfer

<D n="2737" a="1858">
<b>2737.</b> (<b>1858.</b>) Gemeine Menschen werden
durch das heftige Feuer des Ruhmes
Anderer versengt und lassen darum, weil
sie nicht im Stande sind deren Stellung
zu erreichen, ihren Tadel gegen sie aus.
</D>

<D n="2738" a="1125">
<b>2738.</b> (<b>1125.</b>) Zuvorkommenheit gegen die
Seinigen, Mitleid mit Fremden, stete
Falschheit Schlechten gegenüber,
Freundschaft mit Guten, Klugheit Fürsten
gegenüber, Geradheit gegen Gebildete,
Heldenmuth Feinden gegenüber, Nachsicht
mit Eltern, Verschlagenheit Weibern
gegenüber: nur auf Männern, die in
solchen Künsten geschickt sind, beruht
die Welt.
</D>

<D n="2739,2740" a="4160,4161">
<b>2739.</b> <b>2740.</b> (<b>4160.</b> <b>4161.</b>) Folgende
fanden ja den Tod, weil sie sich den
sechs Feinden des Menschen hingegeben
hatten: der Fürst von Dandaka
(Bṛhadaśva) durch Liebe, Ganamegaja
durch Zorn, der königliche Weise
Purūravas durch Habsucht, der Unhold
Vātāpi durch Schadenfreude, der Riese
Rāvaṇa durch Selbstüberschätzung, der
König Dambhodhava durch Hochmuth.

<D n="2746" a="4170">
<b>2746.</b> (<b>4170.</b>) Wenn es Freigebige giebt,
dann bedarf man nicht der Alles
gewährenden Wunderbäume; sind Bettler
da, so braucht man nicht mehr nach Stroh
sich umzusehen; ist ein Blutsverwandter
da, so ist Feuer nicht mehr von Nothen;
ist ein Freund da, so sind himmlische
Kräuter vom Ueberfluss; wenn die
Geliebte uns vor Augen tritt, dann
bedarf es keines mit Kampfer
bestrichenen Pinsels mehr; wenn im Leben
auch ein treues Weib nur eine Art von
Blendwerk ist, dann braucht man auch
dieses nicht mehr.
</D>

<D n="2757" a="1134">

verschenkt und nicht geniesst, dem wird
das dritte Schicksal des Geldes zu
Theil.

Geliebte, bewahren können;

</D>

so beschaffen sein muss, dass ihr
Jedermann beikommen kann und dass sie
von selbst abfällt, darum gewährt eine
solche Frucht, die zu rechter Zeit bei
blosser Berührung abfällt, uns eine
Freude.
</D>
<F n="2846">
2846) YOGAYĀTRĀ 1, 21 in Ind. St.
10, 167.

<info L="2915" page="2.143" gtypes="S,D,F"/>
<S n="2915">
<s>dUrAdutsukamAgate vivalitaM saMBAziRi sPAritaM</s>

</S>
<D n="2915" a="1219">
<b>2915.</b> (<b>1219.</b>) O wie das Auge der mit
dem untreuen Liebsten Schmollenden ein
Meister geworden ist in der Kunst, die
mannichfachsten Formen anzunehmen! Ist
er noch der Ferne, so blickt es
sehnsuchtsvoll; ist er herangetreten, so
wendet es sich zur Seite; redet er sie
an, so thut es sich weit auf; umschlingt
er sie, so wird es roth; ergreift er ihr
Gewand, so runzelt es ein wenig die
Brauenliane; macht er Anstalt sich ihr

Unverdaulichkeit?

<D n="2987" a="4224">

<S n="2999">
<s>drazwavyezu kimuttamaM mfgadfSAM premaprasannaM muKaM</s>

<D n="2999" a="1265">
<b>2999.</b> (<b>1265.</b>) Was verdient vor Allem
gesehen zu werden? Der Rehäugigen vor
Liebe heiter strahlendes Gesicht. Was
gerochen zu werden? Ihres Mundes Athem.
Was gehört zu werden? Ihre Reden. Was
geschmeckt zu werden? Ihrer
Lippenknospen Nass. Was berührt zu
werden? Ihr Leib. Woran sollen
Empfindungsvolle vor Allem denken? An
ihre frische Jugend. Ueberall stehen sie
obenan.
</D>
